	id = daoyu_common.30
	title = daoyu_cheat_menu
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { space_owner = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } } }
}

}

	id = daoyu_common.19

	is_triggered_only = yes

		enable_special_project = { name = "DAOYU_DISBAND_BEHEMOTH_SPECIAL_PROJECT" location = this owner = from }
	}
}

planet_event = {
	id = daoyu_common.21
	title = daoyu_edit_planet#编辑星球
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_target_planet } } save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_planet }
		space_owner = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
}

namespace = daoyu_precursor_1
ship_event = {
	id = daoyu_precursor_1.1
	title = "precursor.1.name"
	desc = "precursor.1.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_archaeological_dig
	location = from
	event_chain = vultaum_chain
	is_triggered_only = yes
	specimen = fossilized_vultaum_remains
	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = vultaum_intro
			begin_event_chain = { event_chain = "vultaum_chain" target = THIS }
			add_event_chain_counter = { event_chain = "vultaum_chain" counter = "vultaum_artifacts" amount = 5 }
			country_event = { id = story.5 days = 30 }
		}
		ship_event = { id = daoyu_precursor_1.2 scopes = { from = from } }
	}
	option = {
		name = INTERESTING
		owner = {
			tooltip = { begin_event_chain = { event_chain = "vultaum_chain" target = THIS } }
			if = { limit = { has_ancrel = yes } small_artifact_reward = yes }
		}
	}
}

			fleet = {
				if = { limit = { not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_precursor_5_leader } } daoyu_create_scientistset = yes last_created_leader = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_precursor_5_leader } assign_leader = event_target:daoyu_precursor_5_leader }
				if = { limit = { or = { not = { exists = leader } and = { exists = leader leader = { not = { is_same_value = event_target:daoyu_precursor_5_leader } } } } } assign_leader = event_target:daoyu_precursor_5_leader }
				set_location = event_target:daoyu_precursor_5_1

		}
		if = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_special_project = CYBREX_HOMEWORLD_PROJECT } } } ship_event = { id = daoyu_precursor_5.4 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu_tech.2
	title = concept_technologies
	desc = daoyu_repeatable_tech
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = daoyu_current_mode
			success_text = { text = MOD_COUNTRY_NUM_TECH_ALTERNATIVES_ADD not = { has_global_flag = SHOW_MORE } }
			success_text = { text = SHOW_MORE has_global_flag = SHOW_MORE }
			text = newline
			text = daoyu_effect_scope
			text = daoyu_repeatable_tech
		}
	}
	diplomatic = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	custom_gui = "formless_diplomacy_window"
	location = capital_scope
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root.ruler
		planet_background = root.owner
		graphical_culture = root.owner
		city_level = root.owner
		room = root.owner
	}
	immediate = { set_global_flag = daoyu_refresh }

		name = daoyu_back

		modify_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species add_trait = trait_robot_suppressed effect = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } }
	}
	option = {
		name = trait_robot_shielded_components#护盾组件
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { is_archetype = ROBOT is_archetype = MACHINE } not = { has_trait = trait_robot_shielded_components } } }
		modify_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species add_trait = trait_robot_shielded_components effect = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } }
	}
	option = {
		name = trait_robot_monoform#单型化
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { is_archetype = ROBOT is_archetype = MACHINE } not = { has_trait = trait_robot_monoform } } }
		modify_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species add_trait = trait_robot_monoform effect = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } }
	}
	option = {
		name = trait_robot_inquisitative_axioms#问询公理
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { is_archetype = ROBOT is_archetype = MACHINE } nor = { has_trait = trait_robot_inquisitative_axioms has_trait = trait_robot_suppressed } } }
		modify_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species add_trait = trait_robot_inquisitative_axioms effect = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } }
	}
	option = {
		name = trait_robot_immortality#永恒机械
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { is_archetype = ROBOT is_archetype = MACHINE } not = { has_trait = trait_robot_immortality } } }
		modify_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species add_trait = trait_robot_immortality effect = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.303 } }
			else = { last_created_species = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } country_event = { id = daoyu_species_traits.1 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu_relic.1
	title = relics
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ADD
		trigger = { daoyu_has_all_relic_trigger = no }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_add_relic
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_relic.2 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DELETE
		trigger = { daoyu_has_relic_trigger = yes }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_add_relic
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_relic.2 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CLOSE
		default_hide_option = yes
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_relic_in_progress
	}
}
